Insert into h_hastakayit_alt_puan
  (id,
   dtype,
   hiid,
   hi_puan,
   ek_etar,
   ek_puan,
   puantype,
   hi_miktar,
   ek_miktar,
   doktorid,
   islemid,
   pers_ekul,
   pers_etar,
   ek_saat, hkid, ek_ekul, hi_sagsol, hi_dis, hi_bolge,genel_anestezi,ozellikli_islem)
  select sqe_h_hastakayit_alt_puan_id.nextval,
         2 as dtype,
         t.hiid,
         case
           when nvl(t.hi_mesaidisi,'H') = 'E' and t.resmikod2 not in  ('520.030','520.033','520.034','520.040','520.041','520.043','520.044') then round( (t.puan ) * 1.2 ,2)
           when nvl(t.hi_mesaidisi,'H') = 'E' and t.resmikod2 in  ('520.030','520.033','520.034','520.040','520.041','520.043','520.044') then round( (t.puan ) * 1.5 ,2)
             else t.puan end as puan,
         trunc(t.tarih),
         case
           when nvl(t.hi_mesaidisi,'H') = 'E' and t.resmikod2 not in  ('520.030','520.033','520.034','520.040','520.041','520.043','520.044') then round( (t.puan ) * 1.2 ,2)
           when nvl(t.hi_mesaidisi,'H') = 'E' and t.resmikod2 in  ('520.030','520.033','520.034','520.040','520.041','520.043','520.044') then round( (t.puan ) * 1.5 ,2)
             else t.puan end as puan,
         decode(nvl(t.hi_mesaidisi,'H'), 'H', '2100', '2200') as puantype,
         t.miktar,
         t.miktar,
         decode(t.doktorid,null,-1,0,-1,'',-1,t.doktorid) as doktorid,
         t.islemid,
         decode(t.doktorid,null,-1,0,-1,'',-1,t.doktorid) as doktorid,
         trunc(t.tarih),
         t.saat,t.hkid,decode(t.doktorid,null,-1,0,-1,'',-1,t.doktorid) as doktorid,
         t.hi_sagsol, t.hi_dis, t.hi_bolge,Decode(t.hi_istemsebebi,' Genel Anestezi Altında',1,0) as Genel_Anestezi,t.is_ozellikliislem
    from v_ist2_ekprim_list t
   where 1=1
     and (select count(*)
            from h_hastakayit_alt_puan ap
           where ap.hiid = t.hiid
             and nvl(ap.doktorid,'-1') = decode(t.doktorid,null,-1,0,-1,'',-1,t.doktorid)) = 0
     and (t.onaydurum=1)
and t.tarih >= :bastarih and t.tarih < :bittarih

call ekprim.procMaxGunlukMiktar(:bastarih,:bittarih)


BASTARIH=['01.05.2024']
BITTARIH=[<Unsupported [0x9C]> ]


Elapsed time: 0.172

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Timestamp: 03.05.2024 13:36:37


BEGIN
FOR AY IN (
SELECT T.ID,
(SELECT  MAX(NVL(ALT.HI_PUAN,0)) * 2 FROM H_HASTAKAYIT_ALT ALT
INNER JOIN H_ISLEM I ON I.IS_ID=ALT.HI_ISLEMID
WHERE ALT.HI_KAYITID=T.hkid
AND substr(nvl(i.gil_resmikod,i.is_resmikod),0,7) IN ('520.020', '520.021', '520.030', '520.031', '520.033', '520.034', '520.035', '520.036', '520.037', '520.038', '520.039', '520.040', '520.041', '520.042', '520.043', '520.044', '520.045')) AS PUAN,
          nvl(T.hi_mesaidisi, 'H') AS MESAIDISI
             FROM V_IST2_EKPRIM_LISTKAYIT T
            INNER JOIN H_ISLEM I
               ON I.IS_ID = T.islemid
            INNER JOIN H_HASTAKAYIT X
               ON X.HK_ID = T.HKID
            WHERE 1 = 1
              AND T.EK_ETAR >=:BASTARIH
              AND T.EK_ETAR < :BITTARIH
              and t.resmikod2 IN ('520.032')
              AND NVL(T.IK_STATUS, 0) = 0
               ) LOOP
  UPDATE H_HASTAKAYIT_ALT_PUAN TT
     SET TT.EK_PUAN     = AY.PUAN,
         TT.EK_ACIKLAMA = 'Mesai saatleri dışında yapılan konsültan hekim muayeneleri bu kapsamda değerlendirilir. İlgili muayene işlem kodu için belirlenen puanın 2 katı esas alınarak puanlandırılır.'
   WHERE TT.ID = AY.ID;
  COMMIT;
END LOOP;
END;

select
count(t.id) as msj,sum(case when t.seviye in (3,4) then 1 else 0 end) as msjsvy
from FONETHBYS.fia_duyuru t
left join FONETHBYS.fia_dagitim d on d.dagitimtur = 2 and d.dagitimrefid = t.id
where durum='+' and (trunc(sysdate-t.tarih) <=gun) and ((d.alicitur = 1 and d.aliciid = :USERID) or
(d.alicitur = 2 and d.aliciid in (select grupid from FONETHBYSADM.ytk_kulgrupuye kgu where kgu.userid = :USERID)))
and (select count(*) from FONETHBYS.fia_dagitimoku do where do.dagitimtur = 2 and do.dagitimrefid = t.id and do.ekul = :USERID) <
(case when (nvl((select max(nvl(dtar,etar)) from FONETHBYS.fia_dagitimoku ok where ok.dagitimrefid = t.id and ok.dagitimtur = 2 and ok.ekul = :USERID),sysdate-1) +
((((t.tarih+(t.gun-1) - t.tarih)*1440)+480)/t.okumasayi)/1440) < sysdate then 2 else 1 end)
 AND t.tarih+t.gun >= (SELECT NVL(ETAR,SYSDATE -1)  FROM FONETHBYSADM.YTK_KULLANICI KUL  WHERE KUL.ID = :USERID)

Timestamp: 03.05.2024 14:04:14


BEGIN
  FOR AY IN (select ID,EK_PUAN+FARK AS TOPLAM from (SELECT T.ID,
                    T.ek_puan,
                    ((SELECT max(VV.ek_puan) * 2
                        FROM v_ist2_ekprim_listkayit VV
                       WHERE VV.hkid = T.hkid
                         AND VV.resmikod2 IN ('520.007','520.008','520.009','520.020','520.021','520.030','520.031','520.033','520.034','520.035',
                                              '520.036','520.037','520.038','520.039','520.040','520.041','520.042','520.043','520.044',
                                              '520.045')) - T.ek_puan) / 2 AS FARK
               FROM V_IST2_EKPRIM_LISTKAYIT T
              INNER JOIN H_ISLEM I
                 ON I.IS_ID = T.islemid
              INNER JOIN H_HASTAKAYIT X
                 ON X.HK_ID = T.HKID
              WHERE 1 = 1
               and t.ek_etar >=:BASTARIH and t.ek_etar < to_date(:BITTARIH)+1
                and t.resmikod2 IN ('520.032')
                AND NVL(T.IK_STATUS, 0) = 0)) LOOP
    UPDATE H_HASTAKAYIT_ALT_PUAN D
       SET D.EK_PUAN =AY.TOPLAM
     WHERE D.ID = AY.ID;
    COMMIT;
  END LOOP;
END;

SELECT
P.ID AS PUANID,
(SELECT I.AYNI_TARAF_KONTROL FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1)  AS AynıTarafKontrol,
(SELECT I.ISLEMID FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1)  AS MasterIslemId,
(SELECT D.ISLEMID FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I, H_BIRKULISLEMDETAY D WHERE D.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND D.UST_ID=I.ID AND ROWNUM =1)  AS MasterDetayIslemId,
(SELECT I.ID FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1) AS MasterUstId,
(SELECT I.ust_id FROM H_BIRKULISLEMDETAY I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1) AS MasterDetayUstId,
P.HKID,
P.HI_SAGSOL,
P.EK_PUAN,
P.EK_ACIKLAMA
FROM H_HASTAKAYIT_ALT_PUAN P WHERE P.EK_ETAR >='01.05.2024' AND P.EK_ETAR<to_date('02.05.2024')+1
   AND P.HI_SAGSOL IS NOT NULL AND P.HKID='45378973'
   ORDER BY HKID

(SELECT I.ISLEMID FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1)  AS MasterIslemId,
(SELECT D.ISLEMID FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I, H_BIRKULISLEMDETAY D WHERE D.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND D.UST_ID=I.ID AND ROWNUM =1)  AS MasterDetayIslemId,

(SELECT I.AYNI_TARAF_KONTROL FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1)  AS AynıTarafKontrol,
(SELECT I.ISLEMID FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1)  AS MasterIslemId,
(SELECT D.ISLEMID FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I, H_BIRKULISLEMDETAY D WHERE D.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND D.UST_ID=I.ID AND ROWNUM =1)  AS MasterDetayIslemId,
(SELECT I.ID FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1) AS MasterUstId,
(SELECT I.ust_id FROM H_BIRKULISLEMDETAY I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1) AS MasterDetayUstId,
P.HKID,
P.HI_SAGSOL,
P.EK_PUAN,
P.EK_ACIKLAMA
FROM H_HASTAKAYIT_ALT_PUAN P WHERE P.EK_ETAR >='01.05.2024' AND P.EK_ETAR<to_date('02.05.2024')+1
   AND P.HI_SAGSOL IS NOT NULL AND P.HKID='45379044'
   ORDER BY HKID


HKID=['45379044']
BASTARIH=['01.05.2024']
BITTARIH=['02.05.2024']


Elapsed time: 0.000

(SELECT I.AYNI_TARAF_KONTROL FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1)  AS AynıTarafKontrol,
(SELECT I.ISLEMID FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1)  AS MasterIslemId,
(SELECT D.ISLEMID FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I, H_BIRKULISLEMDETAY D WHERE D.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND D.UST_ID=I.ID AND ROWNUM =1)  AS MasterDetayIslemId,
(SELECT I.ID FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1) AS MasterUstId,
(SELECT I.ust_id FROM H_BIRKULISLEMDETAY I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1) AS MasterDetayUstId,
P.HKID,
P.HI_SAGSOL,
P.EK_PUAN,
P.EK_ACIKLAMA
FROM H_HASTAKAYIT_ALT_PUAN P WHERE P.EK_ETAR >='01.05.2024' AND P.EK_ETAR<to_date('02.05.2024')+1
   AND P.HI_SAGSOL IS NOT NULL AND P.HKID='45381955'
   ORDER BY HKID


HKID=['45381955']
BASTARIH=['01.05.2024']
BITTARIH=['02.05.2024']


Elapsed time: 0.000

(SELECT I.AYNI_TARAF_KONTROL FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1)  AS AynıTarafKontrol,
(SELECT I.ISLEMID FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1)  AS MasterIslemId,
(SELECT D.ISLEMID FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I, H_BIRKULISLEMDETAY D WHERE D.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND D.UST_ID=I.ID AND ROWNUM =1)  AS MasterDetayIslemId,
(SELECT I.ID FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1) AS MasterUstId,
(SELECT I.ust_id FROM H_BIRKULISLEMDETAY I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1) AS MasterDetayUstId,
P.HKID,
P.HI_SAGSOL,
P.EK_PUAN,
P.EK_ACIKLAMA
FROM H_HASTAKAYIT_ALT_PUAN P WHERE P.EK_ETAR >='01.05.2024' AND P.EK_ETAR<to_date('02.05.2024')+1
   AND P.HI_SAGSOL IS NOT NULL AND P.HKID='45383884'
   ORDER BY HKID


HKID=['45383884']
BASTARIH=['01.05.2024']
BITTARIH=['02.05.2024']


Elapsed time: 0.000

(SELECT I.AYNI_TARAF_KONTROL FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1)  AS AynıTarafKontrol,
(SELECT I.ISLEMID FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1)  AS MasterIslemId,
(SELECT D.ISLEMID FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I, H_BIRKULISLEMDETAY D WHERE D.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND D.UST_ID=I.ID AND ROWNUM =1)  AS MasterDetayIslemId,
(SELECT I.ID FROM H_BIRKULISLEM I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1) AS MasterUstId,
(SELECT I.ust_id FROM H_BIRKULISLEMDETAY I WHERE I.ISLEMID=P.ISLEMID AND ROWNUM =1) AS MasterDetayUstId,
P.HKID,
P.HI_SAGSOL,
P.EK_PUAN,
P.EK_ACIKLAMA
FROM H_HASTAKAYIT_ALT_PUAN P WHERE P.EK_ETAR >='01.05.2024' AND P.EK_ETAR<to_date('02.05.2024')+1
   AND P.HI_SAGSOL IS NOT NULL AND P.HKID='45383612'
   ORDER BY HKID


HKID=['45383612']
BASTARIH=['01.05.2024']
BITTARIH=['02.05.2024']

((((t.tarih+(t.gun-1) - t.tarih)*1440)+480)/t.okumasayi)/1440) < sysdate then 2 else 1 end)

((((t.tarih+(t.gun-1) - t.tarih)*1440)+480)/t.okumasayi)/1440) < sysdate then 2 else 1 end)
 AND t.tarih+t.gun >= (SELECT NVL(ETAR,SYSDATE -1)  FROM FONETHBYSADM.YTK_KULLANICI KUL  WHERE KUL.ID = :USERID)

Timestamp: 03.05.2024 15:33:55

select t.bastarih,
       t.bittarih,
       trunc(t.tarih) as tarih,
       k.adsoyad as kullanici_adi,
       decode(t.type,1,'Aktarım',2,'Silme',3,'İş Kuralları',4,'Agent') as type, to_char(max(t.tarih),'HH24:MI') as saat
  from ist2_ekprim_donem_log t
 inner join FONETHBYSADM.ytk_kullanici k on k.id=t.ekul
 where t.yil=:yil
   and t.donem=:donem group by t.bastarih,t.bittarih,trunc(t.tarih),k.adsoyad,t.type



YIL=['2024']
DONEM=['5']
